### stemmimg
for word in data:
    token_words = word_tokenize(word)
    for i in token_words:
        stem_words = stemmer.stem(i)
        print(stem_words,end = ' ')

#### lemmatizing
for word in data:
    token_words = word_tokenize(word)
    for token in token_words:
        lemma_words = lem.lemmatize(token)
        print(lemma_words,end = ' ')

### name_entity_recognizing

for word in data:
    #print (data)
    named_entity = ne_chunk(pos_tag(word_tokenize(word)))
    print(named_entity)
    #f.write(named_entity)

### 3 -A ####

#f = open('t1.txt','a+')

l = []
for word in data:
    token_words = word_tokenize(word)
    pos = pos_tag(token_words)
    #print(pos)
    for i, j in pos:
        if j=='PRP' or j=='PRP$':
            dat2 = pos[0][0],j
            #print(dat2)
            #dat2.count('tia')
            #print((sum(dat2)))
            l.append(pos[0][0])
            
            
          
### count of num of pronouns 
b = l
for i in set(b):
    x = l.count(i)
    print(i,x)

import pandas as pd
d = {'female': ['julie', 'caroline','tia','judith','rebecca','rita','meg','lynn'],'#prp/prp$':[33,21,86,40,33,67,48,29],
     'male': ['rick', 'matthew','aaron','david','NA','NA','NA','NA'], '#pronouns':[56,1,15,81,0,0,0,0]}

df = pd.DataFrame(data = d)
